package gmrowe.projecteuler

import gmrowe.projecteuler.util.ArrayHelper.binarySearch

case class HandResult(value: Int, description: String)

object PokerEval {
   import Ranks._
   import Suits._

   val handSize: Int = 5       
   
   /**
     Returns an int from 1 to 7462 representing the value of the hand. A score
     of 1 indicates the highest possible hand (Royal Flush) and a score of 7462
     indicates the worst possible hand (75432 unsuited).
   */
   def score(cards: Card*): HandResult = {      
      require(cards.size == handSize)
      
      val codes = cards.map (encode(_))
      
      val upos = (codes.foldLeft (0) ((red, card) => card | red)) >> 16
      
      val res = 
         if (isFlush(codes: _*)) {
            flushes(upos)
         } else if (unique5(upos) != HandValue.Empty){
            unique5(upos)
         } else {
            val primes = codes.map (_ & 0xFF)
            val theCode = primes.reduceLeft (_ * _)
            val idx = binarySearch[HandValue](pairs, theCode == _.code, theCode < _.code)
            pairs(idx.get)
         }
         
      HandResult(res.value, res.description)      
   }
   
   /*Returns true if passed cards all of which are the same suit.*/
   private def isFlush(codes: Int*): Boolean = {
       val reduced = codes.foldLeft (0x0f00) ((red, card) => card & red)
       reduced  != 0
   }
   
               
  /*
     Encodes the card as in Int using the following encoding scheme:
     
         akqjt 98765432
     +--------+--------+--------+--------+
     |xxxrrrrr|rrrrrrrr|xxxxcdhs|xxpppppp|
     +--------+--------+--------+--------+
     p = prime number representing rank of card
     deuce = 2, 
     three = 3,
     four  = 5,
     five  = 7,
     six   = 11, 
     seven = 13,
     eight = 17,
     nine  = 19,
     ten   = 23,
     jack  = 29,
     queen = 31,
     king  = 37,
     ace   = 41
     
     cdhs = bit set to represent suit of card
     r = bit set to represent suit of card
   */
   private def encode(card: Card): Int = {
      
      val rankPrime: Int =
         card.rank match {
            case Deuce => 2
            case Three => 3
            case Four  => 5
            case Five  => 7
            case Six   => 11
            case Seven => 13
            case Eight => 17
            case Nine  => 19
            case Ten   => 23
            case Jack  => 29
            case Queen => 31
            case King  => 37
            case Ace   => 41
        }        
    
      val rankBit: Int =
         card.rank match {
            case Deuce => 0x00010000
            case Three => 0x00020000
            case Four  => 0x00040000
            case Five  => 0x00080000
            case Six   => 0x00100000
            case Seven => 0x00200000
            case Eight => 0x00400000
            case Nine  => 0x00800000
            case Ten   => 0x01000000
            case Jack  => 0x02000000
            case Queen => 0x04000000
            case King  => 0x08000000
            case Ace   => 0x10000000
        }  
      
      val suitBit: Int = 
         card.suit match {
            case Spades   => 0x0100
            case Hearts   => 0x0200
            case Diamonds => 0x0400
            case Clubs    => 0x0800
         }
      
      rankBit | suitBit | rankPrime
   }

   private trait HandValue {
      def value: Int
      def code: Int
      def description: String
      
      override def toString: String = 
           "value=" + value + " code=" + code + " description=" + description
   }
   
   private object HandValue {
   
      def apply(aValue: Int, aCode: Int, aDescription: String): HandValue = {
         new HandValue {
           val value = aValue
           val code = aCode
           val description = aDescription
         }
      }
      
      object Empty extends HandValue {
         def value = 0
         def code = 0
         def description = ""
      }
   }


   private val flushes: Array[HandValue] = 
      FHolder_1() ++ FHolder_2() ++ FHolder_3() ++ FHolder_4() ++
      FHolder_5() ++ FHolder_6() ++ FHolder_7() ++ FHolder_8() ++
      FHolder_9() ++ FHolder_10() ++ FHolder_11() ++ FHolder_12() ++
      FHolder_13() ++ FHolder_14() ++ FHolder_15() ++ FHolder_16() ++

      FHolder_21() ++ FHolder_22() ++ FHolder_23() ++ FHolder_24() ++
      FHolder_25() ++ FHolder_26() ++ FHolder_27() ++ FHolder_28() ++
      FHolder_29() ++ FHolder_30() ++ FHolder_31() ++ FHolder_32()

   private val unique5: Array[HandValue] =
      U5Holder_1() ++ U5Holder_2() ++ U5Holder_3() ++ U5Holder_4() ++
      U5Holder_5() ++ U5Holder_6() ++ U5Holder_7() ++ U5Holder_8() ++

      U5Holder_21() ++ U5Holder_22() ++ U5Holder_23() ++ U5Holder_24() ++
      U5Holder_25() ++ U5Holder_26() ++ U5Holder_27() ++ U5Holder_28() ++
      U5Holder_29() ++ U5Holder_30() ++ U5Holder_31() ++ U5Holder_32()
      
   private val pairs: Array[HandValue] = 
      PHolder_1() ++ PHolder_2() ++ PHolder_3() ++ PHolder_4() ++
      PHolder_5() ++ PHolder_6() ++ PHolder_7() ++ PHolder_8() ++
